     1→/**
     2→ * objects.js — interactive object state machines for the Japanese Home scene.
     3→ *
     4→ * Each object definition has:
     5→ *   { id, name, position: { tx, ty }, interactMs, state, states }
     6→ *
     7→ * Each state can have:
     8→ *   transitions: { use: { next: 'stateName' } }   — triggered by interact()
     9→ *   auto_next:   { state: 'stateName', after: N }  — fires automatically after N seconds
    10→ *   speech:      'string'                           — shown as character speech bubble
    11→ *   emoji:       '🍳'                               — floating emoji on transition
    12→ */
    13→
    14→// ── Object definitions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    15→// Japanese Home (912×642, 19×13 tiles, 48px each).
    16→// Walkable interior: cols 1–17, rows 2–9.
    17→
    18→export const OBJECT_DEFS = [
    19→  {
    20→    id: 'stove',
    21→    name: 'stove',
    22→    position: { tx: 3, ty: 3 },
    23→    interactMs: 8000,
    24→    state: 'idle',
    25→    states: {
    26→      idle: {
    27→        transitions: { use: { next: 'cooking' } },
    28→      },
    29→      cooking: {
    30→        speech: 'Let me cook something...',
    31→        auto_next: { state: 'done', after: 30 },
    32→      },
    33→      done: {
    34→        emoji: '🍳',
    35→        speech: "Dinner's ready! 🍳",
    36→        auto_next: { state: 'idle', after: 60 },
    37→        transitions: { use: { next: 'idle' } },
    38→      },
    39→    },
    40→  },
    41→  {
    42→    id: 'fridge',
    43→    name: 'fridge',

    45→    interactMs: 5000,
    46→    state: 'idle',
    47→    states: {
    48→      idle: {

    50→      },

    52→        speech: 'Hmm, what to eat...',
    53→        auto_next: { state: 'idle', after: 10 },
    54→        transitions: { use: { next: 'idle' } },
    55→      },
    56→    },
    57→  },

   204→];
   205→
   206→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   207→
   208→class ObjectInstance {
   209→  constructor(def) {
   210→    this.id        = def.id;
   211→    this.name      = def.name;
   212→    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   213→    this.position  = def.position;
   214→    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   215→    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   216→    this.states    = def.states;
   217→    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   218→    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   219→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   220→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   221→  }
   222→
   223→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   224→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   225→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   226→  }
   227→
   228→  /**
   229→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   230→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   231→   */
   232→  interact(action = 'use') {
   233→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   234→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   235→    if (!tr) return null;
   236→
   237→    this.state = tr.next;
   238→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   239→
   240→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   241→    return {
   242→      objectId: this.id,
   243→      state:    this.state,
   244→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   245→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   246→    };
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  /**
   250→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   251→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   252→   */
   253→  tick(deltaMs) {
   254→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   255→
   256→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   257→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   258→
   259→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   260→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   261→
   262→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   263→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   264→
   265→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   266→    return {
   267→      objectId: this.id,
   268→      state:    this.state,
   269→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   270→      auto:     true,
   271→    };
   272→  }
   273→}
   274→
   275→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   276→
   277→export class ObjectEngine {
   278→  constructor() {
   279→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  addObjects(defs) {
   283→    for (const def of defs) {
   284→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   285→    }
   286→  }
   287→
   288→  /**
   289→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   290→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   291→   */
   292→  tick(deltaMs) {
   293→    const events = [];
   294→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   295→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   296→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   297→    }
   298→    return events;
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  /**
   302→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   303→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   304→   */
   305→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   306→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   307→  }
   308→
   309→  getAll()   { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   310→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   311→}
   312→

    44→// Rows 0–1 = roof/top wall; rows 10–12 = genkan / exterior — not walkable.
    45→
    46→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    47→  const grid = [];
    48→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    49→    const r = [];
    50→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    51→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    52→    }
    53→    grid.push(r);
    54→  }
    55→  return grid;
    56→}

    60→export class CafeScene extends Phaser.Scene {

   102→      });

   239→  <script type="module">
   240→    import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './src/objects.js';
   241→    import { SimulationEngine } from './src/Engine.js';
   242→    import { Character } from './src/Character.js';
   243→    import { AIEngine } from './src/AIEngine.js';
   244→
   245→    // ── Walkable grid (mirrors scene.js) ──────────────────────────────────────
   246→
   247→    const GRID_COLS = 19;
   248→    const GRID_ROWS = 13;
   249→
   250→    function buildWalkableGrid() {
   251→      const grid = [];
   252→      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
   253→        const r = [];
   254→        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
   255→          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
   256→        }
   257→        grid.push(r);
   258→      }
   259→      return grid;
   260→    }
   261→
   262→    // ── Character definitions (mirrors scene.js) ─────────────────────────────
   263→
   264→    const CHARS_CONFIG = [
   265→      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,
   266→        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },
   267→      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,
   268→        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },
   269→      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 14, ty: 5,
   270→        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },
   271→    ];
   272→
   273→    // ── Engine setup ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   274→
   275→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   276→
   277→    const aiEngine = new AIEngine({
   278→      endpoint: '/api/llm',
   279→      model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   280→      decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,
   281→      onDecision: (char, decision, objects) => {
   282→        const targetName = decision.targetId
   283→          ? (objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId)?.name ?? decision.targetId)
   284→          : decision.targetTile
   285→            ? `(${decision.targetTile.tx},${decision.targetTile.ty})`
   286→            : null;
   287→        pushAILog(char.label, decision.action, targetName, decision.dialogue);
   288→      },
   289→    });
   290→
   291→    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS, aiEngine });
   292→
   293→    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {
   294→      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({
   295→        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   296→      }));
   297→    }
   298→
   299→    // ── UI state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   300→
   301→    let paused = false;
   302→    let speed  = 1;
   303→    let lastTs = null;
   304→
   305→    // Event log (newest-first)
   306→    const log = [];
   307→    const MAX_LOG = 150;
   308→    let logDirty = false;
   309→
   310→    // Track previous object states so we can log from→to
   311→    const prevStateMap = new Map();
   312→    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   313→      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   314→    }
   315→
   316→    // ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   317→
   318→    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
   319→    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   320→      paused = !paused;
   321→      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';
   322→      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);
   323→      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume
   324→    });
   325→
   326→    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
   327→      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   328→        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);
   329→        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   330→        btn.classList.add('active');
   331→      });
   332→    });
   333→
   334→    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
   335→      // Reset object states to defaults
   336→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   337→        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);
   338→        if (!obj) continue;
   339→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';
   340→        obj._resetAutoTimer();
   341→        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);
   342→      }
   343→      // Reset sim clock
   344→      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   345→      // Clear log
   346→      log.length = 0;
   347→      logDirty = true;
   348→      // Update badge classes immediately
   349→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   350→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   351→      }
   352→    });
   353→
   354→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   355→
   356→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   357→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   358→    ]);
   359→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   360→
   361→    function badgeClass(state) {
   362→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   363→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   364→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   365→      return 'other';
   366→    }
   367→
   368→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   369→
   370→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   371→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   372→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   373→      logDirty = true;
   374→    }
   375→
   376→    function pushAILog(charLabel, action, target, dialogue) {
   377→      log.unshift({ type: 'ai', charLabel, action, target, dialogue, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   378→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   379→      logDirty = true;
   380→    }
   381→
   382→    // ── Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) ─────────────────────
   383→
   384→    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {
   385→      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   386→      if (!obj) return;
   387→      const from = obj.state;
   388→      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   389→      if (ev) {
   390→        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);
   391→        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);
   392→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   393→      }
   394→    };
   395→
   396→    // ── Build DOM cards (once) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   397→
   398→    function initObjectCards() {
   399→      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');
   400→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   401→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   402→        card.className = 'object-card';
   403→        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;
   404→        card.innerHTML = `
   405→          <div class="object-card-header">
   406→            <span class="object-name">${obj.name}</span>
   407→            <span class="state-badge" id="badge-${obj.id}"></span>
   408→          </div>
   409→          <div class="position-hint">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>
   410→          <div class="timer-bar" id="timerbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   411→            <div class="timer-fill" id="timerfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   412→          </div>
   413→          <div class="timer-text" id="timertext-${obj.id}" style="display:none"></div>
   414→          <div class="interactions" id="int-${obj.id}"></div>
   415→        `;
   416→        grid.appendChild(card);
   417→        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint
   418→      }
   419→    }
   420→
   421→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   422→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   423→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   424→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   425→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   426→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   427→      if (!badge) return;
   428→
   429→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   430→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   431→
   432→      if (stateChanged) {
   433→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   434→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   435→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   436→
   437→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   438→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   439→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   440→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   441→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   442→        ).join('');
   443→      }
   444→
   445→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   446→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   447→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   448→      if (hasTimer) {
   449→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   450→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   451→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   452→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   453→        timerText.style.display = '';
   454→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   455→      } else {
   456→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   457→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   458→      }
   459→    }
   460→
   461→    function initCharacterCards() {
   462→      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');
   463→      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
   464→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   465→        card.className = 'character-card';
   466→        card.id = `char-${i}`;
   467→        grid.appendChild(card);
   468→        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint
   469→      });
   470→    }
   471→
   472→    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {
   473→      const card = document.getElementById(`char-${i}`);
   474→      if (!card) return;
   475→
   476→      const targetName = char.interactTarget
   477→        ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)
   478→        : char.targetObjectId
   479→          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)
   480→          : '—';
   481→
   482→      // AI decision cooldown timer
   483→      let cooldownHtml = '';
   484→      if (aiEngine.enabled) {
   485→        const remaining  = Math.max(0, aiEngine._timers.get(char.name) ?? aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs);
   486→        const pct        = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - remaining / aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs) * 100));
   487→        const secRemaining = Math.ceil(remaining / 1000);
   488→        cooldownHtml = `
   489→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   490→            <span>AI next</span>
   491→            <span class="char-value">${secRemaining}s</span>
   492→          </div>
   493→          <div class="stat-bar">
   494→            <div class="stat-fill ai-cooldown" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   495→          </div>
   496→        `;
   497→      }
   498→
   499→      card.innerHTML = `
   500→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>
   501→        <div class="char-row">
   502→          <span>Action</span>
   503→          <span class="action-badge ${char.action}">${char.action}</span>
   504→        </div>
   505→        <div class="char-row">
   506→          <span>Position</span>
   507→          <span class="char-value">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>
   508→        </div>
   509→        <div class="char-row">
   510→          <span>Facing</span>
   511→          <span class="char-value">${char.facing}</span>
   512→        </div>
   513→        <div class="char-row">
   514→          <span>Target</span>
   515→          <span class="char-value">${targetName}</span>
   516→        </div>
   517→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   518→          <span>Mood</span>
   519→          <span class="char-value">${char.mood}</span>
   520→        </div>
   521→        <div class="stat-bar">
   522→          <div class="stat-fill mood" style="width:${char.mood}%"></div>
   523→        </div>
   524→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   525→          <span>Energy</span>
   526→          <span class="char-value">${char.energy}</span>
   527→        </div>
   528→        <div class="stat-bar">
   529→          <div class="stat-fill energy" style="width:${char.energy}%"></div>
   530→        </div>
   531→        ${cooldownHtml}
   532→      `;
   533→    }
   534→
   535→    function renderEventLog() {
   536→      if (!logDirty) return;
   537→      logDirty = false;
   538→
   539→      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');
   540→      if (log.length === 0) {
   541→        el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div>';
   542→        return;
   543→      }
   544→      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => {
   545→        if (e.type === 'ai') {
   546→          const targetStr   = e.target   ? ` \u2192 ${e.target}` : '';
   547→          const dialogueStr = e.dialogue ? ` \u201c${e.dialogue}\u201d` : '';
   548→          return `
   549→            <div class="log-entry ai">
   550→              <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   551→              <span class="log-obj">${e.charLabel}</span>
   552→              <span class="log-transition">${e.action}${targetStr}${dialogueStr}</span>
   553→              <span class="log-tag ai">AI</span>
   554→            </div>
   555→          `;
   556→        }
   557→        return `
   558→          <div class="log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}">
   559→            <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   560→            <span class="log-obj">${e.objectId}</span>
   561→            <span class="log-transition">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>
   562→            <span class="log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}">${e.trigger}</span>
   563→          </div>
   564→        `;
   565→      }).join('');
   566→    }
   567→
   568→    // ── Tick loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   569→
   570→    function tick(ts) {
   571→      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   572→
   573→      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {
   574→        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;
   575→
   576→        // Snapshot states before update
   577→        const snap = new Map();
   578→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   579→
   580→        // Advance simulation
   581→        simEngine.update(realDelta);
   582→
   583→        // Detect auto-transitions
   584→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   585→          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {
   586→            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');
   587→            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   588→          }
   589→          updateObjectCard(obj);
   590→        }
   591→
   592→        // Update character cards
   593→        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));
   594→      }
   595→
   596→      lastTs = ts;
   597→
   598→      // Clock
   599→      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();
   600→
   601→      // Event log (only when dirty)
   602→      renderEventLog();
   603→    }
   604→
   605→    // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   606→
   607→    initObjectCards();
   608→    initCharacterCards();
   609→    requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   610→  </script>
   611→</body>
   612→</html>
   613→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #19
Now I understand the issue. Both `debug.html` and `scene.js` have a `buildWalkableGrid()` function that marks all tiles in the rectangle (cols 1-17, rows 2-9) as walkable, but doesn't exclude tiles occupied by objects. The fix needs to: 1. In `buildWalkableGrid()`, after building the base rectangle, mark object tiles as non-walkable 2. Read object positions from `OBJECT_DEFS` to build the exclusion list 3. Apply this fix in BOTH `debug.html` and `scene.js` The object positions that should be non-walkable are: - stove (3,3), fridge (2,3), tea_set (5,5), kotatsu (6,6), tv (9,3) - bookshelf (15,3), desk (14,5), bed (16,5), easel (2,7), bonsai (11,8) These are already defined in `OBJECT_DEFS` in `objects.js`. For `scene.js`, I need to import `OBJECT_DEFS` and iterate through it to mark those positions as non-walkable in the grid. For `debug.html`, `OBJECT_DEFS` is already imported, so I just need to apply the same logic there. The fix involves updating `buildWalkableGrid()` in both files to loop through `OBJECT_DEFS` and set those coordinates as non-walkable. Updating the function...

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer  = 0;
   126→    this.interactTarget = null;
   127→
   128→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   129→    this.mood   = 100;
   130→    this.energy = 100;
   131→
   132→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   133→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   134→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   135→
   136→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   137→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   138→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   139→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   140→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   141→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   142→
   143→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   144→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   145→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   146→
   147→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   148→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   149→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   150→  }
   151→
   152→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   153→
   154→  get px() {
   155→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   156→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   157→    }
   158→    const next = this.path[0];
   159→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   160→  }
   161→
   162→  get py() {
   163→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   164→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   165→    }
   166→    const next = this.path[0];
   167→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   168→  }
   169→
   170→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   171→
   172→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   173→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   174→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   175→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   176→
   177→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   178→      this.path         = path;
   179→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   180→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   181→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   182→      this.action       = 'walking';
   183→
   184→      // Set initial facing from first step
   185→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   186→      this._playWalkAnim();
   187→      return true;
   188→    }
   189→    return false;
   190→  }
   191→
   192→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   193→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   194→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   195→  }
   196→
   197→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   198→    this.action         = 'interacting';
   199→    this.interactTarget = target;
   200→    this.interactTimer  = durationMs;
   201→    if (this.sprite) {
   202→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   203→    }
   204→  }
   205→
   206→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   207→
   208→  update(deltaMs) {
   209→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   210→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   211→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   212→
   213→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   214→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   215→
   216→      // Advance tiles
   217→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   218→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   219→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   220→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   221→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   222→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   224→      }
   225→
   226→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   227→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   228→        this.action       = 'idle';
   229→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   230→        this._playAnim('idle');
   231→      } else {
   232→        this._playWalkAnim();
   233→      }
   234→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   235→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   237→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   239→        this.action        = 'idle';
   240→        this.interactTarget = null;
   241→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   242→        this._playAnim('idle');
   243→      }
   244→    }
   245→
   246→    // Tick dialogue
   247→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   248→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   249→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   250→    }
   251→
   252→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   253→    if (this.sprite) {
   254→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   255→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   256→    }
   257→
   258→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   259→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   260→    }
   261→  }
   262→
   263→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   264→
   265→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   266→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   267→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   268→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   269→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   270→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   271→    });
   272→  }
   273→
   274→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   275→
   276→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   277→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   278→    const next = this.path[0];
   279→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   280→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   281→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   282→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   283→    } else {
   284→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   285→    }
   286→  }
   287→
   288→  _playAnim(type) {
   289→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   290→    const key = type === 'idle'
   291→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   292→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   293→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   294→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   295→    }
   296→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   297→  }
   298→
   299→  _playWalkAnim() {
   300→    this._playAnim('walk');
   301→  }
   302→}
   303→

    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→      });
    56→    }
    57→
    58→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    59→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    60→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    61→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    62→    }
    63→
    64→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    65→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    66→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    67→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    68→      }
    69→
    70→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    72→        this._doWander(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    76→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    77→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    78→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    79→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    80→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    81→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    82→        }
    83→      }
    84→
    85→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    86→      char.update(deltaMs);
    87→    }
    88→  }
    89→
    90→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    91→
    92→  /**
    93→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    94→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    95→   */
    96→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    97→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    98→
    99→    if (event) {
   100→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   101→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000);
   102→
   103→      if (event.speech) {
   104→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   105→      }
   106→
   107→      if (event.emoji) {
   108→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   109→      }
   110→    }
   111→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   112→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   113→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   114→  }
   115→
   116→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   117→
   118→  _doWander(char) {
   119→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   120→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   121→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   122→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   123→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   124→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   125→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   126→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   127→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   128→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   129→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   130→            return;
   131→          }
   132→        }
   133→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   134→      }
   135→    }
   136→
   137→    // Random walkable tile
   138→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   139→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   140→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   141→      return;
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   145→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   146→
   147→    let moved = false;
   148→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   149→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   150→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   151→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   152→      if (moved) break;
   153→    }
   154→
   155→    if (!moved) {
   156→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   157→    }
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  /**
   161→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   162→   */
   163→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   164→    const dirs = [
   165→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   166→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   167→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   168→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   169→    ];
   170→    for (const d of dirs) {
   171→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   172→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   173→      }
   174→    }
   175→    return null;
   176→  }
   177→
   178→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   179→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   180→    const tiles = [];
   181→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   182→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   183→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   184→      }
   185→    }
   186→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   187→    return tiles;
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   191→
   192→  getSimTimeString() {
   193→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   194→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   195→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   196→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   197→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   198→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   199→  }
   200→}
   201→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #47
Good. The `_findAdjacentWalkable` function looks at cardinally adjacent tiles and checks if they're walkable. Since we now mark object tiles as non-walkable, adjacent walkable tiles will be different from the object's tile itself. This is exactly what we need. Note one concern: `_getWalkableTiles()` caches the walkable tiles lazily in `_walkableTiles`. Since `buildWalkableGrid()` returns the grid with object tiles as false, the `_getWalkableTiles()` will correctly build the list without object tiles. Also, one important edge case: Ash's initial tile is (14, 5) which is the same as the desk object (14, 5). So Ash starts on a non-walkable tile—I need to verify the character definitions against the object positions to see if this is actually a problem or if there's something I'm missing about how initial placement works. I'm noticing a critical issue: Ash's starting position at (14, 5) is the exact same tile as the desk. If I mark that tile as non-walkable after the fix, the pathfinding algorithm will immediately fail when checking whether the start position is walkable, which breaks the core requirement that pathfinding still works. I need to move Ash's starting position away from the desk tile at (14, 5) since that will become non-walkable. Looking at the adjacent tiles, (15, 5) to the right of the desk should work as a valid starting position, or I could check (14, 4) above it depending on what other objects are nearby. Actually, rereading the issue more carefully, it's specifically about fixing the pathfinding so characters don't walk through walls—the starting position might not be the core concern here. But if Ash starts on a tile that's marked as non-walkable, that could cause problems with the pathfinding system, so I should move her to an adjacent walkable tile to be safe.
